   conform-action transmit
   exceed-action drop
  !
  set cos 2
 !
 class rpvm_datos_criticos
  bandwidth percent 11
  set cos 2
 !
 class rpvm_business
  bandwidth percent 6
  set cos 2
 !
 class class-default
  bandwidth percent 4
  queue-limit 32 packets
  set cos 1
 !
 end-policy-map
